            //GET URL PARAMETERS/VARIABLES
            function sf_param(parameter) {
            return decodeURIComponent((new RegExp('[?|&]' + parameter + '=' + '([^&;]+?)(&|#|;|$)').exec(location.search) || [, ""])[1].replace(/\+/g, '%20')) || null;
            }
                //set up debug  add ?devMode=true before the # in the url to activate
            showLog = false;
            var consoleHolder = console;
            function debug(bool){
                if(!bool){
                    consoleHolder = console;
                    console = {};
                    console.log = function(){};
                }else
                    showLog = true;
                    console = consoleHolder;
            }
            
            if(sf_param('devMode') == 'true' || sf_param('devmode') == 'true' || sf_param('dev') == 'true' || sf_param('showConsole') == 'true' || sf_param('logging') == 'true'){
                debug(true);
                console.log('%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%\n'+
                            '-----------------------------------\n'+
                            'DEVELOPER MODE ENABLED\n'+
                            '-----------------------------------\n'+
                            'Good job! You enabled developer mode.\n'+
                            'This allows you to view and use console.logs.\n'+
                            'It also allows you to use helpful commands for examble type "pageInfo" into the console and press enter\n'+
                           '%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%\n\n')
            }else{
                debug(false);
            }
            
            var br = '\n===========================================================\n'
            
            if(showLog == true){
               pageInfo = "Title"+br+"Liberty University Christian College Education\n\nDescription"+br+"Get your bachelor's degree and choose from hundreds of graduate degrees including law, medicine, and divinity. Liberty is a Christian university in Central Virginia.\n\n\n\nWindow Size"+br+"("+$(window).width()+" x "+$(window).height()+")";
            }
            
            
            function showMenu(){
            $('.menuBack').fadeIn()
            $('.mobileMenu').css('left','0%');
            $('.mobileMenu').addClass('shown');
            $('.mobileMenu').removeClass('hidden');
            $('.hamMenu').addClass('active')
            $('html').addClass('noScroll');
            }
            function hideMenu(){
            $('.menuBack').fadeOut()
            $('.mobileMenu').css('left','-100%');
            $('.mobileMenu').removeClass('shown');
            $('.mobileMenu').addClass('hidden');
            $('.hamMenu').removeClass('active')
            $('html').removeClass('noScroll')
            goback();
            }
            function goback(){
            $('.mobileMenu .mega').css('right','-100%')
            }
            function getDSTstart(){
                d = new Date(2016, 2, 1, 0, 0, 0, 0);
                var day = 0;
                if (d.getDay() != 0) {
                day = 8-(d.getDay())
                day = day + 7
                d = d.setDate(day)
                DST_start = new Date(d)
                }
            }
            function getDSTend(){
                d = new Date(2016, 10, 1, 0, 0, 0, 0);
                var day = 0;
                if (d.getDay() != 0) {
                day = 8-(d.getDay())
                d = d.setDate(day)
                DST_end = new Date(d)
                }
            }
            function setFooterTime(){
             getDSTstart();
             getDSTend();
            //EST
            clientDate = new Date();
            if(clientDate >= DST_start && clientDate <=DST_end){
                offset = -4;
            }else{
                offset = -5;
            }
            
            utc = clientDate.getTime() + (clientDate.getTimezoneOffset() * 60000);
            serverDate = new Date(utc + (3600000*offset));
            var dt = serverDate
            var hours = dt.getHours();
            //it is pm if hours from 12 onwards
            suffix = (hours >= 12)? 'p.m.' : 'a.m.';
            //only -12 from hours if it is greater than 12 (if not back at mid night)
            hours = (hours > 12)? hours -12 : hours;
            //if 00 then it is 12 am
            hours = (hours == '00')? 12 : hours;
            var minutes = dt.getMinutes();
            minutes = (minutes < 10)? '0'+minutes : minutes;
            var time = hours+':'+minutes+' '+suffix
            $('.realTime').text(time)
            $('#copy_year').html(dt.getFullYear());
            }
            $(document).ready(function(){
            
            setFooterTime();
            setInterval(function(){ setFooterTime(); }, 10000);
            $('.mobileMenu .main_nav .mega .inner .left').prepend('<a href="javascript:goback();">Back</a>')
            $('.mobileMenu .main_nav').click(function(){
                $(this).children('.mega').css('right','0')
            })
            $('.hamMenu').click(function(){
                if($(this).hasClass('active')){
                    hideMenu();
                }else{
                    showMenu();
                }
            });
            $('.menuBack').bind("click",function(){
                hideMenu();
            })
            });
        </script>

                    name = $(this).parents('.cover').siblings('.mainSlide').children().data('cycle-title');
                    dataLayer.push({'event': 'GAevent', 'eventCategory': 'homepageSlides', 'eventAction': 'hpg-prev-click', 'eventLabel': "'"+name+"'"})
                })

                    name = $(this).parents('.cover').siblings('.mainSlide').children().data('cycle-title');

            $('.mobileMenu ul:first').bind('mousewheel DOMMouseScroll', function(e) {
            var scrollTo = null;
            
            if (e.type == 'mousewheel') {
            scrollTo = (e.originalEvent.wheelDelta * -1);
            }
            else if (e.type == 'DOMMouseScroll') {
            scrollTo = 40 * e.originalEvent.detail;
            }
            
            if (scrollTo) {
            e.preventDefault();
            $(this).scrollTop(scrollTo + $(this).scrollTop());
            }
            });
            
            $('.mobileMenu .mega').bind('mousewheel DOMMouseScroll', function(e) {

            function focalPoint($img,x,y){
            if($(window).width() > 1024){
            //console.log('desktop')
            $($img).each(function(){
            picY = $(this).height()/2;
            picX = $(this).width()/2;
            holderY = $('.mainSlide').height()/2;
            availToMoveY = Math.floor(picY - holderY);
            //console.log(picY)
            //console.log(picX)
            //console.log('Focal Point is: '+y)
            focYpx = (picY*2)*y;
            posFromCenter = Math.floor(focYpx - picY);
            // console.log('From Center: '+posFromCenter)
            if(posFromCenter > 0){
            //console.log("Focal Point is in the lower half of the image")
            if(posFromCenter > availToMoveY){
            //console.log($(this))
            //console.log('margin-top'+(availToMoveY-13)*-1+'px')
            $(this).css('margin-top',(availToMoveY-13)*-1+'px');
            }else{
            //console.log('margin-top'+(posFromCenter-13)*-1+'px')
            $(this).css('margin-top',(posFromCenter-13)*-1+'px')
            }
            }else{
            //console.log("Focal Point is in the upper half of thr image")
            if((posFromCenter*-1) > availToMoveY){
            //console.log($(this))
            //console.log('margin-top'+(availToMoveY-13)+'px')
            $(this).css('margin-top',(availToMoveY-13)+'px');
            }else{
            //console.log('margin-top'+(posFromCenter-13)*-1+'px')
            $(this).css('margin-top',(posFromCenter-13)*-1+'px')
            }
            }
            })
            }
            }

            all, for now. 1 at a time can be a future optimization

            jQuery.support.cors = true; // Fix IE bug loading XML via AJAX
            
            function openGallery(galleryID){
            $('.exploreSlide img').remove();
            $('.exploreSlide #exploreSlides').children().remove()
            $('.exploreSlide #exploreSlides').html('');
            $('.exploreSlide').append('<div class="loading" style="width:900px;height:600px;background:#E1E1E1;"><div class="sk-circle"><div class="sk-circle1 sk-child"></div><div class="sk-circle2 sk-child"></div><div class="sk-circle3 sk-child"></div><div class="sk-circle4 sk-child"></div><div class="sk-circle5 sk-child"></div><div class="sk-circle6 sk-child"></div><div class="sk-circle7 sk-child"></div><div class="sk-circle8 sk-child"></div><div class="sk-circle9 sk-child"></div><div class="sk-circle10 sk-child"></div><div class="sk-circle11 sk-child"></div><div class="sk-circle12 sk-child"></div></div></div>')
            
            $.ajax({
            url: galleryURL + galleryID,
            dataType: 'xml',
            crossDomain: true,
            success: function(xml) {
            
            var count = 1;
            var len = $(xml).find('image').length;
            var imageArrayStr = '';
            $(xml).find('image').each(function(){
            
            var title = $(this).find('title').text();
            var url = $(this).find('image_url').text();
            //not using descriptions anymore, just un-needed content to maintain
            // var description = $(this).find('description').text();
            var description = count + ' of ' + len;
            //console.log(url)
            //console.log(description)
            //console.log(title)
            if(count === 1){
                $('.exploreSlide').prepend('<img src="'+url+'"/>');
            }else{
                if(count === 2){
                    imageArrayStr = '[ ';
                }
                if(count < len){
                imageArrayStr += '"<img src=\''+url+'\'>", ';
                }else{
                    imageArrayStr += '"<img src=\''+url+'\'>"';
                    imageArrayStr += ' ]';
                }
            }
            
            //    console.log('Count: ' + count + ' - Len: ' + len);
            count++;
            
            });
            $('.exploreSlide #exploreSlides').html(imageArrayStr);
                console.log(imageArrayStr);
            
            $('.exploreSlide').cycle('reinit');
            
            },
            error: function(message,error,type){
            console.log(error + " " + type);
            //output a 'refresh your browser' msg to user
            
            }
            });
            }
            
            
            
            //  THIS CODE MIGHT NOT BE NEEDED ANYMORE......YES YES IT IS
            
            $( '.mainSlide' ).on( 'cycle-before', function( event, opts ) {
            $('.slideInfo').css('opacity','0')
            setTimeout( function(){
            $('.slideInfo').css('opacity','1')
            },650);
            });
            
            
            $( '.mainSlide' ).on( 'cycle-next', function( event, opts ) {
            console.log('next')
            $('.slideInfo').css('opacity','0')
            setTimeout( function(){
            $('.slideInfo').css('opacity','1')
            },650);
            });
            
            $( '.mainSlide' ).on( 'cycle-prev', function( event, opts ) {
            console.log('prev')
            $('.slideInfo').css('opacity','0')
            setTimeout( function(){
            $('.slideInfo').css('opacity','1')
            },650);
            });
        </script>
